## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes CronJob v1beta1 to batch/v1 Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement CronJob API handling for both v1beta1 and batch/v1: the conversion functions, the TimeZone field addition in v1, the validation changes, and the defaulting logic differences between versions.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

```json
{

  ],

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Summary of CronJob v1beta1 to batch/v1 Migration Files

### Conversion Functions
The conversion between v1beta1 ↔ internal and v1 ↔ internal is handled by:
- **`pkg/apis/batch/v1beta1/zz_generated.conversion.go`**: Auto-generated functions like `Convert_v1beta1_CronJob_To_batch_CronJob`, `Convert_batch_CronJob_To_v1beta1_CronJob`, and spec/status/list variants. The TimeZone field is copied via `unsafe.Pointer` (zero-copy).
- **`pkg/apis/batch/v1/zz_generated.conversion.go`**: Same pattern for v1 ↔ internal conversion.
- **`pkg/apis/batch/v1beta1/conversion.go`** and **`pkg/apis/batch/v1/conversion.go`**: Manual conversion registration (field labels, JobSpec helpers).

### TimeZone Field Addition in v1
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/api/batch/v1/types.go`**: External v1 `CronJobSpec` with `TimeZone *string`
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/api/batch/v1beta1/types.go`**: External v1beta1 `CronJobSpec` also has `TimeZone` (marked as replacement=batch,v1,CronJob)
- **`pkg/apis/batch/types.go`**: Internal hub type with `TimeZone *string`

### Validation Changes
- **`pkg/apis/batch/validation/validation.go`**: `validateTimeZone()` validates timezone names; only triggered when the field changes (immutability-like behavior on update).

### Defaulting Logic Differences
- **`pkg/apis/batch/v1beta1/defaults.go`**: Uses `new(bool)` for Suspend
- **`pkg/apis/batch/v1/defaults.go`**: Uses `ptr.To(false)` for Suspend (functionally equivalent but idiomatic v1 style)

### Strategy (v1beta1 vs v1 behavior)
- **`pkg/registry/batch/cronjob/strategy.go`**: Returns `OrphanDependents` for batch/v1beta1 (backward compat) vs `DeleteDependents` for v1; defines reset fields for both versions.
